Infrastructure** (`staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/`)\\n\\nKubernetes builds a custom metrics stability framework on top of `prometheus/client_golang`. The core is in:\\n\\n- `registry.go`: Defines the `KubeRegistry` interface and `kubeRegistry` struct. The `kubeRegistry` wraps a `prometheus.Registry` (via the `PromRegistry` interface defined in `wrappers.go`) and adds Kubernetes-specific features: metric versioning/deprecation lifecycle, hidden metric management, and resettable metrics. Key symbols: `NewKubeRegistry`, `Registerable` (interface that all k8s metrics must implement, extending `prometheus.Collector`), `KubeRegistry` (interface with `Register`, `MustRegister`, `CustomRegister`, `CustomMustRegister`, `RawMustRegister`), `RegisterMetaMetrics` (registers meta-metrics like `registered_metrics_total`, `disabled_metrics_total`, `hidden_metrics_total`).\\n\\n- `legacyregistry/registry.go`: Provides the **global singleton registry** used by almost all Kubernetes components. Key globals: `defaultRegistry` (a `KubeRegistry` created at package init), `DefaultGatherer`, `MustRegister`, `Register`, `RawMustRegister`, `CustomRegister`, `CustomMustRegister`. The `Handler()` function creates an HTTP handler using `promhttp.InstrumentMetricHandler` + `promhttp.HandlerFor(defaultRegistry, ...)`, and `HandlerWithReset()` supports DELETE-triggered resets. In `init()`, the process collector, Go runtime collector, and meta-metrics are registered.\\n\\n- `wrappers.go`: Defines reusable interfaces (`Collector`, `Metric`, `CounterMetric`, `GaugeMetric`, `Registerer`, `PromRegistry`) that wrap prometheus types to prevent upstream API breakage.\\n\\n**HTTP Endpoint Registration** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/routes/metrics.go`)\\n\\nThe `DefaultMetrics` struct (with `Install(*mux.PathRecorderMux)`) mounts `legacyregistry.Handler()` at `/metrics`. `MetricsWithReset` mounts `legacyregistry.HandlerWithReset()` at `/metrics`. The `register()` helper registers sub-system metrics (apiserver, cacher, etcd3, flowcontrol, peerproxy, handlers metrics) into the legacy registry.\\n\\n**SLI Metrics** (`staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/prometheus/slis/routes.go`)\\n\\n`SLIMetrics` and `SLIMetricsWithReset` install a separate `/metrics/slis` endpoint using a dedicated `Registry` (separate from the default), demonstrating Kubernetes's multi-registry pattern.\\n\\n**Metric Registration Pattern**: Kubernetes components typically call `legacyregistry.MustRegister(metric)` from package-level `init()` functions (e.g., all etcd vendor metrics), or call a `Register()` function that wraps `legacyregistry.Register`. The stability framework intercepts registration to check if a metric is deprecated/hidden for the current Kubernetes version.\\n\\n---\\n\\n### Grafana\\n\\n**Registry Infrastructure** (`pkg/infra/metrics/`)\\n\\nGrafana uses `prometheus/client_golang` more directly, with a dependency injection pattern via Wire:\\n\\n- `metrics.go`: Defines all global metric variables (counters, gauges, summaries, histograms) with package-level `var` declarations, initialized in `init()` using standard prometheus constructors (`prometheus.NewCounter`, `prometheus.NewGaugeVec`, etc.). All metrics use `ExporterName = \\\"grafana\\\"` as namespace. The `initMetricVars(reg prometheus.Registerer)` function calls `reg.MustRegister(...)` with all defined metrics. `SetBuildInformation` and `SetEnvironmentInformation` are utility functions that create and register ephemeral metrics.\\n\\n- `service.go`: Central service providing the DI wiring. `ProvideService(cfg, reg)` calls `initMetricVars(reg)` and `initFrontendMetrics(reg)` to register all metrics. `ProvideRegisterer()` returns `legacyregistry.Registerer()` (Kubernetes's legacy registry is reused as the global registerer). `ProvideGatherer()` creates a `multiRegistry` combining an `addPrefixWrapper` (which prefixes non-`grafana_`/`go_` k8s metrics with `grafana_`) around the k8s legacy registry gatherer, plus `prometheus.DefaultGatherer`. This unified gatherer is what gets exposed at `/metrics`.\\n\\n- `frontendmetrics.go`: `initFrontendMetrics(r)` registers histogram metrics for frontend performance timings using `registerFrontendHistogram`.\\n\\n- `settings.go`: Handles optional Graphite bridge configuration for pushing metrics to Graphite via `graphitebridge.NewBridge`.\\n\\n- `wireset.go`: Wire dependency injection set: `WireSet` exposes `ProvideService`, `ProvideRegisterer`, `ProvideGatherer`.\\n\\n- `metricutil/utils.go`: Helpers `NewCounterStartingAtZero` and `NewCounterVecStartingAtZero` initialize counters pre-seeded at zero for label consistency.\\n\\n**HTTP Endpoint** (`pkg/api/http_server.go`)\\n\\nThe `HTTPServer.metricsEndpoint` method (registered as a web middleware via `m.Use(hs.metricsEndpoint)`) handles `GET /metrics`. It checks `hs.Cfg.MetricsEndpointEnabled`, optionally enforces HTTP basic auth, and then calls `promhttp.HandlerFor(hs.promGatherer, promhttp.HandlerOpts{EnableOpenMetrics: true}).ServeHTTP(...)`. The `promGatherer` is the `multiRegistry` provided by `ProvideGatherer()`. The `HTTPServer` also holds a `promRegister` (used by `middleware.RequestMetrics` for HTTP request instrumentation).\\n\\n---\\n\\n### Key Differences\\n\\n1. **Registry abstraction**: Kubernetes wraps prometheus in a full `KubeRegistry` abstraction with versioning/deprecation lifecycle management; Grafana uses prometheus types directly.\\n\\n2. **Global vs. DI**: Kubernetes uses a global package-level `defaultRegistry` in `legacyregistry`; Grafana uses Wire dependency injection to pass `prometheus.Registerer` and `prometheus.Gatherer` through the service graph.\\n\\n3. **Multi-gatherer**: Grafana's `ProvideGatherer()` builds a `multiRegistry` that merges the Kubernetes legacy registry (with a `grafana_` prefix wrapper) and the prometheus default registry—enabling it to expose both Grafana-specific and runtime metrics from a unified `/metrics` endpoint.\\n\\n4. **Endpoint mounting**: Kubernetes mounts `/metrics` via an `Install()` method on a `PathRecorderMux` (declarative route registration); Grafana handles it as a low-level web middleware that intercepts matching requests before routing.\\n\\n5. **Metric collectors**: Kubernetes uses `StableCollector` (a custom interface for complex collectors with hidden/deprecated metric support via `CustomRegister`/`CustomMustRegister`); Grafana uses standard `prometheus.Collector` implementations.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1324,"cache_read_input_tokens":76249,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":1324,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"0525022b-d745-45e3-918d-ffecf849363b","uuid":"caa3010a-54e6-46a4-8f8c-4b704a5f5259"}

`prometheus/client_golang`. The core is in:\\n\\n- `registry.go`: Defines the `KubeRegistry` interface and `kubeRegistry` struct. The `kubeRegistry` wraps a `PromRegistry` (defined in `wrappers.go` as a subset of `prometheus.Registerer`+`prometheus.Gatherer`) and adds Kubernetes-specific features: metric versioning/deprecation lifecycle, hidden metric management, and resettable metrics. Key symbols: `NewKubeRegistry` (creates a new registry backed by `prometheus.NewRegistry()`), `Registerable` (interface that all k8s metrics must implement, extending `prometheus.Collector` with `Create`, `ClearState`, `FQName`), `KubeRegistry` (interface with `Register`, `MustRegister`, `CustomRegister`, `CustomMustRegister`, `RawMustRegister`), `RegisterMetaMetrics` (registers meta-metrics: `registered_metrics_total`, `disabled_metrics_total`, `hidden_metrics_total`, `cardinality_enforcement_unexpected_categorizations_total`).\\n\\n- `legacyregistry/registry.go`: Provides the **global singleton registry** used by almost all Kubernetes components. Key globals: `defaultRegistry` (a `KubeRegistry` created at package init via `metrics.NewKubeRegistry()`), `DefaultGatherer`, `MustRegister`, `Register`, `RawMustRegister`, `CustomRegister`, `CustomMustRegister`. The `Handler()` function creates an HTTP handler using `promhttp.InstrumentMetricHandler` + `promhttp.HandlerFor(defaultRegistry, promhttp.HandlerOpts{ProcessStartTime: processStart})`. `HandlerWithReset()` wraps a handler that also supports DELETE-triggered registry resets. In `init()`, the process collector, Go runtime collector (with all runtime metrics), and meta-metrics are registered via `RawMustRegister` and `RegisterMetaMetrics`.\\n\\n- `wrappers.go`: Defines reusable interfaces (`Collector`, `Metric`, `CounterMetric`, `GaugeMetric`, `Registerer`, `PromRegistry`) that wrap prometheus types for API stability.\\n\\n**HTTP Endpoint Registration** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/routes/metrics.go`)\\n\\nThe `DefaultMetrics` struct (with `Install(*mux.PathRecorderMux)`) mounts `legacyregistry.Handler()` at `/metrics`. `MetricsWithReset` mounts `legacyregistry.HandlerWithReset()` at `/metrics`. The `register()` helper registers apiserver, cacher, etcd3, flowcontrol, peerproxy, and handlers metrics into the legacy registry before mounting.\\n\\n**SLI Metrics** (`staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/prometheus/slis/routes.go`)\\n\\n`SLIMetrics` and `SLIMetricsWithReset` install a separate `/metrics/slis` endpoint using a dedicated `Registry` (separate from the default), demonstrating Kubernetes's multi-endpoint pattern.\\n\\n**Metric Registration Pattern**: Kubernetes components call `legacyregistry.MustRegister(metric)` from package-level `init()` functions, or call a `Register()` function that wraps `legacyregistry.Register`. The stability framework intercepts registration to check if a metric is deprecated/hidden for the current Kubernetes version, hiding it if appropriate.\\n\\n---\\n\\n### Grafana (sg-evals/grafana--v11.4.0)\\n\\n**Registry Infrastructure** (`pkg/infra/metrics/`)\\n\\nGrafana uses `prometheus/client_golang` more directly, with a Wire dependency injection pattern:\\n\\n- `metrics.go`: Defines all global metric variables (counters, gauges, summaries, histograms) as package-level `var` declarations, all initialized in `init()` using standard prometheus constructors (`prometheus.NewCounter`, `prometheus.NewGaugeVec`, `prometheus.NewSummary`, `prometheus.NewHistogram`, etc.). All metrics use `ExporterName = \\\"grafana\\\"` as namespace. The `initMetricVars(reg prometheus.Registerer)` function bulk-registers all metrics via `reg.MustRegister(...)`. `SetBuildInformation` and `SetEnvironmentInformation` create and register additional labeled gauge metrics at runtime.\\n\\n- `service.go`: The central DI-wired service. `ProvideService(cfg, reg)` calls `initMetricVars(reg)` and `initFrontendMetrics(reg)` to register all metrics. `ProvideRegisterer()` returns `legacyregistry.Registerer()` (Kubernetes's k8s.io/component-base legacy registry is reused as the global registerer, allowing Kubernetes runtime metrics to also appear). `ProvideGatherer()` creates a `multiRegistry` combining an `addPrefixWrapper` (which prefixes non-`grafana_`/`go_` k8s metrics with `grafana_`) around the k8s legacy registry gatherer, plus `prometheus.DefaultGatherer`. This unified multi-gatherer is what gets exposed at `/metrics`.\\n\\n- `frontendmetrics.go`: `initFrontendMetrics(r)` registers histogram metrics for frontend performance timings (boot time, first paint, JS/CSS load) via `registerFrontendHistogram`.\\n\\n- `settings.go`: Handles optional Graphite bridge configuration for pushing metrics to Graphite via `graphitebridge.NewBridge`.\\n\\n- `wireset.go`: Wire DI set exporting `ProvideService`, `ProvideRegisterer`, `ProvideGatherer`.\\n\\n- `metricutil/utils.go`: Helpers `NewCounterStartingAtZero` and `NewCounterVecStartingAtZero` initialize counters pre-seeded at zero for label consistency across label value sets.\\n\\n**HTTP Endpoint** (`pkg/api/http_server.go`)\\n\\nThe `HTTPServer.metricsEndpoint` method (registered as a web middleware at line 637 via `m.Use(hs.metricsEndpoint)`) handles `GET /metrics`. It checks `hs.Cfg.MetricsEndpointEnabled`, optionally enforces HTTP basic auth, then calls `promhttp.HandlerFor(hs.promGatherer, promhttp.HandlerOpts{EnableOpenMetrics: true}).ServeHTTP(...)`. The `promGatherer` is the `multiRegistry` from `ProvideGatherer()`. The `HTTPServer` also holds `promRegister` used by `middleware.RequestMetrics` for per-request HTTP instrumentation.\\n\\n---\\n\\n### Key Differences\\n\\n1. **Registry abstraction**: Kubernetes wraps prometheus in a `KubeRegistry` abstraction with versioning/deprecation lifecycle management; Grafana uses prometheus types directly.\\n\\n2. **Global vs. DI**: Kubernetes uses a global package-level `defaultRegistry` in `legacyregistry`; Grafana uses Wire DI to pass `prometheus.Registerer` and `prometheus.Gatherer` through the service graph.\\n\\n3. **Multi-gatherer**: Grafana's `ProvideGatherer()` builds a `multiRegistry` merging the Kubernetes legacy registry (with a `grafana_` prefix wrapper for non-prefixed metrics) and `prometheus.DefaultGatherer`—enabling a unified `/metrics` exposition from both registries.\\n\\n4. **Endpoint mounting**: Kubernetes mounts `/metrics` via an explicit `Install()` method on `PathRecorderMux` (declarative); Grafana handles it as a low-level web middleware intercepting matching requests.\\n\\n5. **Collector registration**: Kubernetes uses `StableCollector` for complex collectors with hidden/deprecated metric support via `CustomRegister`/`CustomMustRegister`; Grafana uses standard `prometheus.Collector` implementations with a helper utility (`metricutil`) for zero-seeded counters.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":3,"cache_creation_input_tokens":355,"cache_read_input_tokens":81833,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":355,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"0525022b-d745-45e3-918d-ffecf849363b","uuid":"a06ce9f3-df6e-4aa6-8d5a-1dc1ae4f10a7"}

(sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0)\\n\\n**Registry Infrastructure** (`staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/`)\\n\\nKubernetes builds a custom metrics stability framework on top of `prometheus/client_golang`. The core is in:\\n\\n- `registry.go`: Defines the `KubeRegistry` interface and `kubeRegistry` struct. The `kubeRegistry` wraps a `PromRegistry` (defined in `wrappers.go` as a subset of `prometheus.Registerer`+`prometheus.Gatherer`) and adds Kubernetes-specific features: metric versioning/deprecation lifecycle, hidden metric management, and resettable metrics. Key globals: `defaultRegistry` (a `KubeRegistry` created at package init via `metrics.NewKubeRegistry()`), `DefaultGatherer`, `MustRegister`, `Register`, `RawMustRegister`, `CustomRegister`, `CustomMustRegister`. The `Handler()` function creates an HTTP handler using `promhttp.InstrumentMetricHandler` + `promhttp.HandlerFor(defaultRegistry, promhttp.HandlerOpts{ProcessStartTime: processStart})`. `HandlerWithReset()` wraps a handler that also supports DELETE-triggered registry resets. In `init()`, the process collector, Go runtime collector (with all runtime metrics), and meta-metrics are registered via `RawMustRegister` and `RegisterMetaMetrics`.\\n\\n- `wrappers.go`: Defines reusable interfaces (`Collector`, `Metric`, `CounterMetric`, `GaugeMetric`, `Registerer`, `PromRegistry`) that wrap prometheus types for API stability.\\n\\n**HTTP Endpoint Registration** (`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/routes/metrics.go`)\\n\\nThe `DefaultMetrics` struct (with `Install(*mux.PathRecorderMux)`) mounts `legacyregistry.Handler()` at `/metrics`. `MetricsWithReset` mounts `legacyregistry.HandlerWithReset()` at `/metrics`. The `register()` helper registers apiserver, cacher, etcd3, flowcontrol, peerproxy, and handlers metrics into the legacy registry before mounting.\\n\\n**SLI Metrics** (`staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/prometheus/slis/routes.go`)\\n\\n`SLIMetrics` and `SLIMetricsWithReset` install a separate `/metrics/slis` endpoint using a dedicated `Registry` (separate from the default), demonstrating Kubernetes's multi-endpoint pattern.\\n\\n**Metric Registration Pattern**: Kubernetes components call `legacyregistry.MustRegister(metric)` from package-level `init()` functions, or call a `Register()` function that wraps `legacyregistry.Register`. The stability framework intercepts registration to check if a metric is deprecated/hidden for the current Kubernetes version, hiding it if appropriate.\\n\\n---\\n\\n### Grafana (sg-evals/grafana--v11.4.0)\\n\\n**Registry Infrastructure** (`pkg/infra/metrics/`)\\n\\nGrafana uses `prometheus/client_golang` more directly, with a Wire dependency injection pattern:\\n\\n- `metrics.go`: Defines all global metric variables (counters, gauges, summaries, histograms) as package-level `var` declarations, all initialized in `init()` using standard prometheus constructors (`prometheus.NewCounter`, `prometheus.NewGaugeVec`, `prometheus.NewSummary`, `prometheus.NewHistogram`, etc.).
